{
  "content": "# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer API Reference Documentation\n\n## Overview\n\nThe `KafkaConsumer` is a client for consuming messages from Apache Kafka topics. It transparently handles broker failures and topic partition migration while managing consumer group coordination for load-balanced consumption. The consumer maintains TCP connections to brokers and must be properly closed to avoid resource leaks.\n\n**Thread Safety Model**: The KafkaConsumer is **NOT thread-safe**. All network I/O occurs in the thread making the call. The only thread-safe method is `wakeup()`, which can safely interrupt blocking operations from external threads.\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Core Consumer Lifecycle](#core-consumer-lifecycle)\n2. [Subscription and Assignment Methods](#subscription-and-assignment-methods)\n3. [Polling and Data Fetching](#polling-and-data-fetching)\n4. [Offset Management](#offset-management)\n5. [Consumer Group Mechanics](#consumer-group-mechanics)\n6. [Flow Control and Position Management](#flow-control-and-position-management)\n7. [Metadata and Monitoring](#metadata-and-monitoring)\n8. [Error Handling](#error-handling)\n9. [Core Types and Interfaces](#core-types-and-interfaces)\n10. [Configuration-Driven Behaviors](#configuration-driven-behaviors)\n11. [Common Patterns and Best Practices](#common-patterns-and-best-practices)\n\n---\n\n## Core Consumer Lifecycle\n\n### Constructors\n\n#### `KafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)`\nCreates a consumer with a configuration map. Configuration keys are documented in `ConsumerConfig`.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `configs`: Map of configuration key-value pairs\n\n**Throws:**\n- `KafkaException`: If consumer construction fails (invalid configuration, missing deserializers, etc.)\n\n**Note**: After creating a consumer, you **must** call `close()` to avoid resource leaks.\n\n#### `KafkaConsumer(Properties properties)`\nCreates a consumer with a Properties object.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `properties`: Properties object containing configuration\n\n**Note**: See `ConsumerConfig` for valid configuration strings.\n\n#### `KafkaConsumer(Properties properties, Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer, Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)`\nCreates a consumer with Properties and explicit deserializers.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `properties`: Configuration properties\n- `keyDeserializer`: Custom deserializer for keys (won't be configured via property)\n- `valueDeserializer`: Custom deserializer for values\n\n**Note**: When deserializers are provided directly, their `configure()` method is not called by the consumer.\n\n#### `KafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs, Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer, Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)`\nCreates a consumer with a config map and explicit deserializers.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `configs`: Configuration map\n- `keyDeserializer`: Custom key deserializer\n- `valueDeserializer`: Custom value deserializer\n\n### Lifecycle Methods\n\n#### `void close()`\nCloses the consumer with a default 30-second timeout. Ensures offsets are committed (if enabled) and network connections are cleaned up.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Triggers rebalance listener's `onPartitionsRevoked()` for graceful cleanup\n- Commits pending auto-commit offsets (if enabled)\n- Closes all broker connections\n- Prevents further consumer operations\n\n**Note**: Safe to call multiple times.\n\n#### `void close(Duration timeout)`\nCloses the consumer with a custom timeout.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `timeout`: Maximum duration to wait for graceful shutdown\n\n**Throws:**\n- `TimeoutException`: If graceful shutdown cannot complete within the timeout\n\n#### `void wakeup()`\nThread-safe method to interrupt blocking operations (typically `poll()`).\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Can be called from any thread\n- Causes the blocked thread to throw `WakeupException`\n- Does not cause consumer closure; the consumer remains open for further calls\n\n**Use Case**: Implementing graceful shutdown by calling `wakeup()` from a shutdown hook or signal handler.\n\n---\n\n## Subscription and Assignment Methods\n\n### Dynamic Subscription\n\n#### `void subscribe(Collection<String> topics)`\nSubscribes to a fixed set of topics. Uses a no-op rebalance listener.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `topics`: Collection of topic names to subscribe to\n\n**Throws:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If topics is null or empty\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `assign()` was previously called without `unsubscribe()`\n- `IllegalStateException`: If no partition assignment strategies are configured\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Topics can contain regular characters; special characters may require escaping\n- Partition assignment happens dynamically through configured partition assignors\n- When subscribed topics' partitions change (e.g., scaling), a rebalance is triggered\n- The consumer automatically joins the group on first `poll()` call\n\n#### `void subscribe(Collection<String> topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)`\nSubscribes to topics with custom rebalance callbacks.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `topics`: Collection of topic names\n- `listener`: Custom `ConsumerRebalanceListener` for partition assignment changes\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n- `onPartitionsRevoked()` is called during rebalance before partitions are revoked\n- `onPartitionsAssigned()` is called after partition assignment completes\n- For eager rebalancing: revoked is called at rebalance start\n- For cooperative rebalancing: revoked only called if partitions are actually revoked\n\n**Important**: Rebalance callbacks execute during `poll()` and may block longer than the poll timeout.\n\n#### `void subscribe(Pattern pattern)`\nSubscribes to all topics matching a regex pattern.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `pattern`: Regex pattern for topic names (uses `java.util.regex.Pattern`)\n\n**Metadata Refresh:**\n- Pattern matching is evaluated periodically (controlled by `metadata.max.age.ms`)\n- When new topics matching the pattern are created, a rebalance is triggered\n- When topics are deleted, a rebalance may be triggered\n\n#### `void subscribe(Pattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)`\nSubscribes to pattern-matching topics with custom rebalance listener.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `pattern`: Regex pattern for topic names\n- `listener`: Custom rebalance listener\n\n**Throws:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If pattern is null or empty string\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `assign()` was previously called\n\n### Manual Assignment\n\n#### `void assign(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nManually assigns specific partitions to this consumer. Disables group coordination and rebalancing.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partitions`: Collection of `TopicPartition` objects to assign\n\n**Throws:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If partitions is null or contains null/empty topics\n- `IllegalStateException`: If `subscribe()` was previously called without `unsubscribe()`\n\n**Behavioral Notes:**\n- **No group management**: Manual assignment does not use group coordination\n- **No rebalancing**: Partitions will not be reassigned on consumer failures or new consumers\n- **Explicit responsibility**: The application is responsible for managing offset initialization and commit logic\n- **Static assignment**: Good for applications with fixed partition assignments or external coordination systems\n\n**Offset Management:**\n- When manually assigning, you typically need to manage offset initialization yourself\n- Use `seek()` to set initial positions or `committed()` to fetch previously committed offsets\n\n#### `void unsubscribe()`\nClears all topic subscriptions and manual partition assignments.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Leaves the consumer group (if using group management)\n- Removes all assigned partitions\n- Triggers `onPartitionsRevoked()` on the rebalance listener\n- Subsequent `poll()` calls will raise `IllegalStateException`\n\n**Use Case:** Dynamically switching between topic/partition management strategies.\n\n### Querying Current Assignments\n\n#### `Set<String> subscription()`\nReturns the currently subscribed topics.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Unmodifiable set of subscribed topic names\n- Empty set if using manual assignment or unsubscribed\n- Pattern matches are **not** expanded; returns the original pattern (implementation detail may vary)\n\n#### `Set<TopicPartition> assignment()`\nReturns the currently assigned partitions.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Unmodifiable set of `TopicPartition` objects\n- Empty set if no partitions are assigned\n- Same as input for manual `assign()`; dynamically assigned for `subscribe()`\n\n**Note**: For subscribed topics, this may be empty during rebalancing or if the group hasn't joined yet.\n\n---\n\n## Polling and Data Fetching\n\n#### `ConsumerRecords<K, V> poll(Duration timeout)`\nFetches records from the assigned topics/partitions.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `timeout`: Maximum duration to wait for records (must not exceed `Long.MAX_VALUE` milliseconds)\n\n**Returns:**\n- `ConsumerRecords` containing fetched records, organized by partition\n- Empty `ConsumerRecords` if no data available after timeout\n\n**Throws:**\n- `InvalidOffsetException`: If offset is undefined/out-of-range and no reset policy configured\n- `WakeupException`: If `wakeup()` called before or during poll\n- `InterruptException`: If thread interrupted during poll\n- `CommitFailedException`: If pending auto-commit fails (group rebalanced)\n- `AuthenticationException`: If authentication fails\n- `AuthorizationException`: If lacking read access to subscribed topics\n- `FencedInstanceIdException`: If consumer instance fenced by broker\n- `IllegalStateException`: If consumer not subscribed to any topics/partitions\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If timeout is negative\n\n**Behavioral Semantics:**\n\n1. **Blocking Behavior:**\n   - Returns immediately if records are available in buffer\n   - Otherwise blocks up to `timeout` duration\n   - **May block longer than timeout** if rebalance callbacks are executing\n   - During rebalance, `onPartitionsRevoked()` and `onPartitionsAssigned()` execute within poll()\n\n2. **Rebalance Triggers:**\n   - Rebalances only occur during `poll()` calls\n   - Not during `commit()`, `seek()`, or other API calls\n   - If max.poll.interval.ms expires between polls, consumer is proactively removed from group\n   - Subsequent poll will fail with `CommitFailedException` on commit attempts\n\n3. **Position Updates:**\n   - Consumed position automatically advances as records are returned\n   - Position is independent of committed offset\n   - Position can be queried with `position(TopicPartition)`\n\n4. **Timeout Semantics:**\n   - Specifies maximum time to wait for **broker data** fetches\n   - Does not bound rebalance callback execution\n   - `Duration.ZERO` returns immediately with any available data\n\n5. **Record Ordering:**\n   - Records are ordered by offset within each partition\n   - Records from different partitions are unordered relative to each other\n   - No ordering guarantees across multiple `poll()` calls\n\n---\n\n## Offset Management\n\n### Offset Concepts\n\n**Three key offset concepts:**\n\n1. **Current Position** (`position()`): The offset of the next record to be fetched\n   - Automatically advanced by `poll()`\n   - Can be set via `seek()`\n   - Should be one ahead of the last consumed record\n\n2. **Committed Offset** (`committed()`): Last offset persisted to the broker\n   - Retrieved from broker on startup/rebalance\n   - Set by `commitSync()` or `commitAsync()`\n   - Provides crash recovery point\n\n3. **Lag**: Difference between end offset and current position\n   - Indicates how far consumer is behind\n\n**Important Invariant**: For correctness, the committed offset should always be the offset of the next message the application will consume (i.e., lastConsumedOffset + 1). This ensures no messages are skipped on recovery.\n\n### Automatic Offset Commit\n\n**Configuration:**\n- `enable.auto.commit`: Whether to automatically commit offsets (default: true)\n- `auto.commit.interval.ms`: Frequency of auto-commits (default: 5000 ms)\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Consumer automatically commits position on a periodic interval\n- Happens asynchronously in the background\n- Commit happens before joining a rebalance\n- If enabled, commit failures are logged but not propagated to application\n\n### Manual Offset Commit - Synchronous\n\n#### `void commitSync()`\nSynchronously commits the current position for all assigned partitions.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Blocks until commit succeeds, fails, or times out\n- Commits the position (offset of next record to fetch) for all partitions\n- Uses `default.api.timeout.ms` for timeout\n\n**Throws:**\n- `CommitFailedException`: Consumer no longer part of group (rebalanced)\n- `RebalanceInProgressException`: Rebalance in progress, retry after `poll()`\n- `TimeoutException`: Timeout exceeded\n- `AuthorizationException`: Not authorized to the group\n\n#### `void commitSync(Duration timeout)`\nSynchronously commits with custom timeout.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `timeout`: Custom timeout duration\n\n#### `void commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets)`\nSynchronously commits specific offsets for specific partitions.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `offsets`: Map of `TopicPartition` to `OffsetAndMetadata` pairs\n\n**Important Notes:**\n- Offset should be the next message to consume (lastConsumed + 1)\n- For group-managed subscriptions, offsets must be for currently assigned partitions\n- Allows fine-grained control over which partitions' offsets to commit\n\n**Example:**\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n    // Process records\n    if (!partitionRecords.isEmpty()) {\n        long lastOffset = partitionRecords.get(partitionRecords.size() - 1).offset();\n        consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n            partition,\n            new OffsetAndMetadata(lastOffset + 1)\n        ));\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### `void commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Duration timeout)`\nSynchronously commits specific offsets with custom timeout.\n\n### Manual Offset Commit - Asynchronous\n\n#### `void commitAsync()`\nAsynchronously commits current position for all partitions without callback.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Returns immediately\n- Commit happens in background\n- Errors are logged but not propagated\n- Useful for best-effort commits\n\n#### `void commitAsync(OffsetCommitCallback callback)`\nAsynchronously commits with callback.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `callback`: `OffsetCommitCallback` to invoke when commit completes\n\n**Callback Signature:**\n```java\nvoid onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Exception exception)\n```\n\n**Callback Execution:**\n- Called after broker responds (success or failure)\n- Executed in consumer thread (not background thread)\n- All pending async callbacks execute before `commitSync()` returns\n\n#### `void commitAsync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, OffsetCommitCallback callback)`\nAsynchronously commits specific offsets with callback.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `offsets`: Map of partition to offset+metadata\n- `callback`: Callback invoked when commit completes\n\n**Ordering Guarantees:**\n- Multiple async commits are sent in order of invocation\n- Callbacks are invoked in same order\n- All async callbacks complete before any `commitSync()` returns\n\n### Querying Committed Offsets\n\n#### `OffsetAndMetadata committed(TopicPartition partition)`\nFetches the committed offset for a partition.\n\n**Returns:**\n- `OffsetAndMetadata` containing offset and metadata\n- `null` if no offset committed for partition\n\n**Throws:**\n- `TimeoutException`: Broker request timeout\n\n#### `OffsetAndMetadata committed(TopicPartition partition, Duration timeout)`\nFetches committed offset with custom timeout.\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nFetches committed offsets for multiple partitions.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Map of partitions to committed offsets\n- Partitions with no committed offset are omitted from map\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)`\nFetches committed offsets with custom timeout.\n\n### Position Control\n\n#### `long position(TopicPartition partition)`\nGets the current position (offset of next record to fetch).\n\n**Returns:**\n- Offset of next message to be fetched\n- One more than the last consumed offset\n\n**Note**: This is always available; position is never `null`.\n\n#### `long position(TopicPartition partition, Duration timeout)`\nGets position with custom timeout.\n\n#### `void seek(TopicPartition partition, long offset)`\nSets the position to a specific offset.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partition`: Partition to seek in\n- `offset`: Target offset (must be non-negative)\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Next `poll()` will fetch from this offset\n- Position is not validated against log start/end offsets\n- Allows replaying records or skipping ahead\n\n**Throws:**\n- `IllegalArgumentException`: If offset is negative\n- `IllegalStateException`: If partition not assigned to consumer\n\n#### `void seek(TopicPartition partition, OffsetAndMetadata offsetAndMetadata)`\nSeeks with `OffsetAndMetadata` (includes optional leader epoch).\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partition`: Partition to seek\n- `offsetAndMetadata`: Offset with optional metadata and leader epoch\n\n#### `void seekToBeginning(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nSeeks all specified partitions to the earliest available offset.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partitions`: Collection of partitions to seek\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Seeks to log start offset\n- Takes effect on next `poll()`\n- Useful for replaying historical data\n\n**Note**: Earliest available offset may be after absolute offset 0 due to log retention/cleanup.\n\n#### `void seekToEnd(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nSeeks to the end of partitions (high watermark or LSO).\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partitions`: Collection of partitions\n\n**Behavior:**\n- For `read_uncommitted` isolation: seeks to high watermark\n- For `read_committed` isolation: seeks to Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Takes effect on next `poll()`\n- Useful for consuming only new messages\n\n### Timestamp-based Offset Lookup\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch)`\nFinds offsets closest to specified timestamps.\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `timestampsToSearch`: Map of partition to target timestamp (milliseconds)\n\n**Returns:**\n- Map of partition to `OffsetAndTimestamp` pair\n- Partitions with no matching timestamp return `null` entry\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Finds offset of first message **on or after** the timestamp\n- Requires brokers to have message timestamps\n- Uses log retention to determine available timestamps\n- Returns the earliest offset if requested timestamp is before all messages\n\n**Use Cases:**\n- \"Start consuming from yesterday\"\n- Time-windowed consumption\n- Temporal analysis\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch, Duration timeout)`\nTimestamp lookup with custom timeout.\n\n### Beginning and End Offsets\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nGets the earliest offset available in each partition.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Map of partition to beginning offset\n- Beginning offset may be > 0 due to log compaction or retention\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)`\nBeginning offsets with custom timeout.\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nGets the end offset (high watermark or LSO) for each partition.\n\n**Returns:**\n- For `read_uncommitted`: Returns high watermark (HWM)\n- For `read_committed`: Returns Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- Offset that is **not yet available** for consumption\n\n**Note**: Next offset to fetch would be the offset returned by `endOffsets()`.\n\n#### `Map<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)`\nEnd offsets with custom timeout.\n\n---\n\n## Consumer Group Mechanics\n\n### Consumer Groups and Rebalancing\n\n**Group Membership:**\n- Consumers with the same `group.id` form a group\n- Kafka automatically distributes partitions across group members\n- Each partition is assigned to exactly one consumer in the group\n\n**Rebalance Triggers:**\n1. New consumer joins the group\n2. Consumer leaves the group (via `unsubscribe()` or timeout)\n3. Consumer fails (heartbeat timeout)\n4. Subscribed topics' partitions change (scaling, new topic created)\n5. Subscribed regex matches new topics\n\n**Rebalance Detection:**\n- Only detected during `poll()` calls\n- If `max.poll.interval.ms` expires without `poll()`, consumer is proactively ejected\n\n### Rebalance Listener\n\n#### Interface: `ConsumerRebalanceListener`\n\nCallbacks for handling partition assignment changes:\n\n#### `void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nCalled when partitions are being revoked (gracefully).\n\n**When Called:**\n- Before partitions are revoked from this consumer\n- **Guaranteed to be called before new consumer's `onPartitionsAssigned()`**\n- Happens during `poll()` call\n\n**Purpose:**\n- Save consumed offsets before losing partitions\n- Flush any in-flight processing\n- Clean up partition-specific state\n\n**Example:**\n```java\npublic void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    consumer.commitSync(); // Save offsets\n    cache.clear(); // Clear partition-specific caches\n}\n```\n\n#### `void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nCalled after partitions have been assigned to this consumer.\n\n**When Called:**\n- After rebalance completes\n- Before consumer starts fetching\n- Always called (even with empty partition list to signal rebalance completion)\n- Happens during `poll()` call\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `partitions`: Partitions **newly assigned** (not all assigned partitions)\n\n**Purpose:**\n- Initialize positions for new partitions\n- Load partition-specific state from external store\n- Set up monitoring or metrics\n\n**Example:**\n```java\npublic void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n        long offset = loadOffsetFromExternalStore(partition);\n        consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### `default void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nCalled when partitions are lost ungracefully.\n\n**When Called:**\n- Consumer no longer owns partition due to:\n  - Session timeout (heartbeat missed)\n  - Rebalance exception\n  - Other fatal errors\n- Default implementation calls `onPartitionsRevoked()`\n\n**Purpose:**\n- Different from `onPartitionsRevoked()` because partitions may already be owned by others\n- **Do not commit offsets** for lost partitions (will fail)\n- Clean up resources\n\n**Example:**\n```java\npublic void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n    // Don't try to commit - we no longer own these partitions\n    offlineCache.invalidate();\n}\n```\n\n**Rebalancing Strategies:**\n\n1. **Eager Rebalancing** (default `RangeAssignor`, `RoundRobinAssignor`):\n   - All consumers revoke all partitions at rebalance start\n   - Then all consumers are assigned new partitions\n   - Higher latency, complete pause during rebalance\n\n2. **Cooperative Rebalancing** (`CooperativeStickyAssignor`):\n   - Only revoke partitions that must change\n   - Keep other partitions assigned\n   - Multiple rounds if assignment is complex\n   - Lower latency, some consumption continues\n\n### Group Metadata\n\n#### `ConsumerGroupMetadata groupMetadata()`\nReturns metadata about the consumer's group membership.\n\n**Returns:**\n- `ConsumerGroupMetadata` containing:\n  - Group ID\n  - Generation ID (incremented on rebalance)\n  - Member ID\n  - Used for transactional messages\n\n**Note**: Generation ID changes on every rebalance; useful for detecting rebalance events.\n\n### Rebalance Control\n\n#### `void enforceRebalance()`\nRequests a rebalance on the next `poll()` call.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Consumer initiates rebalance without waiting for timeout\n- Useful for graceful redistribution of load\n- Triggers callbacks on next poll\n\n**Use Case:** Manual load balancing or coordinated shutdown.\n\n---\n\n## Flow Control and Position Management\n\n### Pause and Resume\n\n#### `void pause(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nPauses fetching from specified partitions.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- `poll()` will not return records from paused partitions\n- Records already fetched remain available for processing\n- Useful for rate limiting or waiting for external systems\n\n**Use Cases:**\n- Rate limiting consumer throughput\n- Implementing backpressure when downstream system is slow\n- Decoupling consumption from processing in multi-threaded setup\n\n#### `void resume(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)`\nResumes fetching from previously paused partitions.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Partitions resume fetching on next `poll()`\n- If no partitions are paused, has no effect\n\n#### `Set<TopicPartition> paused()`\nReturns currently paused partitions.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Unmodifiable set of paused `TopicPartition` objects\n\n### Current Lag\n\n#### `OptionalLong currentLag(TopicPartition partition)`\nReturns the current lag for a partition.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Number of records between current position and end offset\n- `OptionalLong.empty()` if lag cannot be determined (e.g., partition not assigned)\n- Does not block; uses cached metadata\n\n**Lag Calculation:**\n- For `read_uncommitted`: `(highWatermark - position)`\n- For `read_committed`: `(LSO - position)`\n- Negative lag indicates consumer is ahead (shouldn't happen)\n\n---\n\n## Metadata and Monitoring\n\n### Partition Metadata\n\n#### `List<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic)`\nGets partition metadata for a topic.\n\n**Returns:**\n- List of `PartitionInfo` containing:\n  - Partition ID\n  - Leader broker\n  - In-sync replicas\n  - All replicas\n\n**Throws:**\n- `TimeoutException`: Metadata fetch timeout\n\n#### `List<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic, Duration timeout)`\nPartition metadata with custom timeout.\n\n#### `Map<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics()`\nGets partition metadata for all topics.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Map of topic name to partition info list\n- Empty map if no topics exist\n- May trigger metadata refresh\n\n**Note**: Includes internal topics unless excluded via `exclude.internal.topics` config.\n\n#### `Map<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics(Duration timeout)`\nAll topics metadata with custom timeout.\n\n### Metrics\n\n#### `Map<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics()`\nReturns metrics kept by the consumer.\n\n**Returns:**\n- Map of `MetricName` to `Metric` objects\n- Includes:\n  - Fetch metrics (records/bytes/time)\n  - Commit metrics (success rate, latency)\n  - Consumer lag metrics\n  - Network I/O metrics\n\n**Use Cases:**\n- Monitoring consumer health\n- Alerting on lag exceeding thresholds\n- Debugging performance issues\n\n---\n\n## Core Types and Interfaces\n\n### ConsumerRecord<K, V>\n\nRepresents a single message consumed from Kafka.\n\n**Key Methods:**\n- `String topic()`: Topic name\n- `int partition()`: Partition number\n- `long offset()`: Offset in partition\n- `long timestamp()`: Message timestamp (milliseconds)\n- `TimestampType timestampType()`: Type of timestamp (CreateTime, LogAppendTime, NoTimestampType)\n- `K key()`: Message key (nullable)\n- `V value()`: Message content\n- `Headers headers()`: Record headers (name-value pairs)\n- `int serializedKeySize()`: Size of serialized key in bytes (-1 if null)\n- `int serializedValueSize()`: Size of serialized value (-1 if null)\n- `Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch()`: Leader epoch (for log truncation detection)\n\n**Offset Semantics:**\n- Offset uniquely identifies record within partition\n- Position after consuming this record is `offset + 1`\n- Not directly comparable across partitions\n\n### ConsumerRecords<K, V>\n\nContainer for records returned by `poll()`.\n\n**Key Methods:**\n- `List<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(TopicPartition partition)`: Records for specific partition\n- `Iterable<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(String topic)`: Records for topic (all partitions)\n- `Set<TopicPartition> partitions()`: Partitions with data\n- `Iterator<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> iterator()`: Iterate all records\n- `int count()`: Total number of records\n- `boolean isEmpty()`: Check if empty\n\n**Iteration:**\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n// Iterate all records\nfor (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n    process(record);\n}\n\n// Iterate per-partition\nfor (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n    List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n    // Commit offsets for partition after processing\n}\n\n// Iterate per-topic\nfor (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records.records(\"my-topic\")) {\n    process(record);\n}\n```\n\n### OffsetAndMetadata\n\nEncapsulates offset and application-provided metadata for commits.\n\n**Constructor Overloads:**\n- `OffsetAndMetadata(long offset)`: Just offset\n- `OffsetAndMetadata(long offset, String metadata)`: Offset with metadata string\n- `OffsetAndMetadata(long offset, Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch, String metadata)`: Full form with leader epoch\n\n**Methods:**\n- `long offset()`: Get committed offset\n- `String metadata()`: Get metadata string (non-null, empty if not provided)\n- `Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch()`: Get optional leader epoch\n\n**Usage:**\n```java\n// Commit offset 100 with metadata\nconsumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n    partition,\n    new OffsetAndMetadata(100, \"processed-up-to-time-\" + System.currentTimeMillis())\n));\n```\n\n### OffsetAndTimestamp\n\nPair of offset and timestamp for timestamp-based offset lookups.\n\n**Methods:**\n- `long offset()`: Offset of message at or after timestamp\n- `long timestamp()`: Actual timestamp of the found message\n- `Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch()`: Optional leader epoch\n\n### ConsumerRebalanceListener (Interface)\n\nSee [Rebalance Listener](#rebalance-listener) section above.\n\n### TopicPartition\n\nIdentifies a specific partition in a topic.\n\n**Constructor:**\n```java\nTopicPartition partition = new TopicPartition(\"my-topic\", 0);\n```\n\n**Methods:**\n- `String topic()`: Topic name\n- `int partition()`: Partition number\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### CommitFailedException\n\n**Cause:** Synchronous commit fails because consumer is no longer part of the group.\n\n**Scenario:**\n- Time between polls exceeds `max.poll.interval.ms`\n- Consumer was fenced by broker\n- Group rebalanced and partitions reassigned\n\n**Recovery:**\n- Do not retry immediately; call `poll()` first\n- Check if partitions still assigned\n- May need to update application state if partitions changed\n\n**Example:**\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Consumer no longer in group; need to rejoin via poll()\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ZERO);\n    // Now attempt recovery logic\n}\n```\n\n### InvalidOffsetException (Abstract Base)\n\nBase for offset-related exceptions.\n\n**Subtypes:**\n1. **NoOffsetForPartitionException**: No committed offset exists and no reset policy configured\n2. **OffsetOutOfRangeException**: Offset beyond broker's range and no reset policy configured\n\n### NoOffsetForPartitionException\n\n**Cause:** No offset committed and `auto.offset.reset` is `none`.\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- First time consumer starts (no previous commits)\n- Consumer restarted after retention period expired\n- Partition reassigned to new consumer and no initial seek\n\n**Resolution:**\n- Change `auto.offset.reset` to `earliest` or `latest`\n- Explicitly call `seek()` with initial offset\n- Implement `ConsumerRebalanceListener.onPartitionsAssigned()` to initialize positions\n\n### OffsetOutOfRangeException\n\n**Cause:** Seeking or position points to offset beyond partition's range.\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Log compaction removed offsets\n- Log retention deleted old records\n- Manually seeked beyond current end\n\n**Resolution:**\n- Seek to `beginningOffsets()` or `endOffsets()`\n- Adjust consumption logic to handle missing records\n- Implement appropriate offset reset strategy\n\n### LogTruncationException\n\n**Cause:** Unclean leader election caused log truncation, breaking offset continuity.\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Thrown during fetch if committed offset is beyond truncation point\n- Contains map of divergent offsets per partition\n\n**Recovery:**\n```java\ncatch (LogTruncationException e) {\n    Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = e.divergentOffsets();\n    for (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n        TopicPartition partition = entry.getKey();\n        OffsetAndMetadata offset = entry.getValue();\n        // Reset to a safe offset\n        consumer.seek(partition, Math.max(offset.offset(), beginingOffsets.get(partition)));\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### WakeupException\n\n**Cause:** `wakeup()` was called while blocking in `poll()` or another operation.\n\n**Handling:**\n```java\ntry {\n    ConsumerRecords records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(10));\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    // Consumer was woken up; exit gracefully\n    return;\n}\n```\n\n### Other Exceptions\n\n- **AuthenticationException**: Authentication failed (invalid credentials)\n- **AuthorizationException**: Not authorized to read topic/group\n- **TimeoutException**: Operation timeout exceeded\n- **FencedInstanceIdException**: Consumer instance with same ID already exists\n- **InvalidTopicException**: Topic name contains invalid characters\n- **RecordDeserializationException**: Deserializing key/value failed\n- **InterruptException**: Thread was interrupted\n- **RebalanceInProgressException**: Rebalance in progress (temporary, can retry)\n\n---\n\n## Configuration-Driven Behaviors\n\n### Essential Configurations\n\n| Config | Type | Default | Behavior |\n|--------|------|---------|----------|\n| `group.id` | String | \"\" | Consumer group ID (required for group management) |\n| `bootstrap.servers` | String | - | Broker addresses for initial connection |\n| `key.deserializer` | Class | - | Deserializer class for record keys |\n| `value.deserializer` | Class | - | Deserializer class for record values |\n| `enable.auto.commit` | Boolean | true | Automatically commit offsets periodically |\n| `auto.commit.interval.ms` | Int | 5000 | Frequency of auto-commits (ms) |\n| `max.poll.interval.ms` | Int | 300000 | Max time between polls before ejection (ms) |\n| `max.poll.records` | Int | 500 | Max records returned per poll() |\n| `session.timeout.ms` | Int | 45000 | Session timeout for heartbeats (ms) |\n| `heartbeat.interval.ms` | Int | 3000 | Heartbeat frequency (ms) |\n| `auto.offset.reset` | String | \"latest\" | Action when offset not found: `earliest`, `latest`, `none` |\n| `isolation.level` | String | \"read_uncommitted\" | `read_committed` for transactional messages |\n| `fetch.min.bytes` | Int | 1 | Min bytes broker waits to return from fetch |\n| `fetch.max.wait.ms` | Int | 500 | Max time broker waits for fetch.min.bytes |\n| `max.partition.fetch.bytes` | Int | 1048576 | Max bytes per partition per fetch (1MB) |\n| `partition.assignment.strategy` | List | [RangeAssignor, CooperativeStickyAssignor] | Partition assignor strategies |\n| `metadata.max.age.ms` | Int | 300000 | Max age of metadata before refresh (5 min) |\n\n### Auto Offset Reset Policy\n\n- **`earliest`**: Start from log beginning (first available offset)\n- **`latest`**: Start from log end (latest offset + 1, no historical data)\n- **`none`**: Throw exception when no offset found\n\n### Isolation Levels\n\n- **`read_uncommitted`** (default): Read all messages (including aborted transactions)\n- **`read_committed`**: Only read committed messages, filter aborted transactions\n\n### Multi-threaded Processing Configuration\n\nFor decoupled consumption and processing:\n- Reduce `max.poll.records` to limit batch size\n- Increase `max.poll.interval.ms` to allow processing time\n- Consider increasing `session.timeout.ms` slightly for GC pauses\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Basic Polling with Auto-Commit\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"true\");\nprops.setProperty(\"auto.commit.interval.ms\", \"1000\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.printf(\"offset = %d, key = %s, value = %s%n\",\n                record.offset(), record.key(), record.value());\n        }\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Simple use cases without complex processing\n- Acceptable to re-process messages on failure (at-least-once)\n- Processing is fast\n\n### Pattern 2: Manual Offset Commit After Batch Processing\n\n```java\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        // Process all records\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n\n        // Commit offsets after batch processed\n        try {\n            consumer.commitSync();\n        } catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n            log.error(\"Commit failed; consumer may have been rebalanced\", e);\n            // Rebalance happened; next poll() will have new assignments\n        }\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Processing is atomic and consistent\n- Need to ensure no offset commits if processing fails\n- Acceptable to re-process on consumer failure\n\n### Pattern 3: Rebalance Listener with External Offset Storage\n\n```java\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"), new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Save offsets before losing partitions\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets = new HashMap<>();\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            offsets.put(partition, new OffsetAndMetadata(\n                consumer.position(partition)\n            ));\n        }\n        externalOffsetStore.saveOffsets(offsets);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Load offsets from external store\n        Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets =\n            externalOffsetStore.loadOffsets(partitions);\n        for (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n            consumer.seek(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().offset());\n        }\n    }\n});\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Offsets stored in external system (database, cache)\n- Need exactly-once semantics with offset commit in same transaction\n- Custom offset logic\n\n### Pattern 4: Decoupled Consumption and Processing\n\n```java\nBlockingQueue<ConsumerRecords> queue = new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(100);\nAtomicBoolean stopped = new AtomicBoolean(false);\n\n// Consumer thread\nThread consumerThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    try {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n        while (!stopped.get()) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records =\n                consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n            if (!records.isEmpty()) {\n                queue.put(records);\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        consumer.close();\n    }\n});\n\n// Processing thread pool\nExecutorService processorPool = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(4);\nfor (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {\n    processorPool.submit(() -> {\n        try {\n            while (!stopped.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = queue.poll(100, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);\n                if (records != null) {\n                    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                        processRecord(record);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n    });\n}\n\n// Graceful shutdown\nRuntime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(() -> {\n    stopped.set(true);\n    consumer.wakeup();\n    processorPool.shutdown();\n    processorPool.awaitTermination(30, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n}));\n\nconsumerThread.start();\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Processing is slow or variable\n- Need parallelism across partitions\n- Can tolerate some latency\n\n### Pattern 5: Seeking and Position Control\n\n```java\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(topicPartition));\n\n// Seek to beginning\nconsumer.seekToBeginning(Arrays.asList(topicPartition));\n\n// Or seek to specific offset\nconsumer.seek(topicPartition, 1000);\n\n// Or seek by timestamp\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets =\n    consumer.offsetsForTimes(Collections.singletonMap(\n        topicPartition,\n        System.currentTimeMillis() - TimeUnit.HOURS.toMillis(24) // 24 hours ago\n    ));\nconsumer.seek(topicPartition, offsets.get(topicPartition).offset());\n\n// Fetch from the position\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Time-windowed consumption\n- Replaying historical data\n- Manual partition management\n\n### Pattern 6: Graceful Shutdown\n\n```java\nAtomicBoolean running = new AtomicBoolean(true);\n\nThread consumerThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    try {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"my-topic\"));\n        while (running.get()) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records =\n                consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(1000));\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                processRecord(record);\n            }\n        }\n    } catch (WakeupException e) {\n        // Ignore wakeup exception\n    } finally {\n        consumer.close();\n    }\n});\n\n// Shutdown hook\nRuntime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(() -> {\n    running.set(false);\n    consumer.wakeup(); // Interrupt blocking poll\n    try {\n        consumerThread.join(30000); // Wait for thread to finish\n    } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n    }\n}));\n\nconsumerThread.start();\n```\n\n**When to Use:**\n- Clean shutdown from signal handlers\n- Multi-threaded consumer architectures\n- Resource cleanup requirements\n\n### Avoiding Common Pitfalls\n\n1. **Not Closing the Consumer**: Always close in finally block or try-with-resources\n2. **Exceeding max.poll.interval.ms**: Keep polling frequency high; move processing to separate thread if needed\n3. **Committing Before Processing**: Ensure processing completes before committing offsets\n4. **Mixing subscribe() and assign()**: Cannot use both; must unsubscribe() first\n5. **Forgetting offset semantics**: Committed offset should be next offset to consume\n6. **Not handling WakeupException**: Must catch and handle gracefully for shutdown\n7. **Blocking rebalance callbacks**: Keep rebalance listener logic fast\n8. **Ignoring rebalance events**: Must be aware partitions may change mid-processing\n\n---\n\n## Threading and Concurrency\n\n### Thread-Safety Rules\n\n- **NOT thread-safe**: Consumer instance, poll(), commit(), seek(), assign(), subscribe()\n- **Thread-safe**: wakeup() only\n\n### Multi-threaded Consumption Strategies\n\n**1. One Consumer Per Thread**\n- Simplest approach\n- Each thread owns its consumer instance\n- Good for low latency\n- Limited by number of partitions\n\n**2. Single Consumer, Multiple Processors**\n- One thread consumes, buffers to queue\n- Multiple processor threads pull from queue\n- Decouples consumption from processing\n- Handles variable processing latency\n\n**3. Per-Partition Processing**\n- Manually assign specific partitions to consumers\n- Each consumer thread processes one or more partitions\n- Maintains per-partition ordering\n- Requires external coordination\n\n---\n\n## Transactional Message Consumption\n\n### Reading Committed Messages Only\n\nSet `isolation.level=read_committed`:\n\n```java\nprops.setProperty(\"isolation.level\", \"read_committed\");\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n- Only reads messages committed by transactional producers\n- Filters out messages from aborted transactions\n- Position limited to Last Stable Offset (LSO)\n- May see gaps in offsets due to transaction markers\n\n---\n\n## Version Compatibility\n\n- Supports brokers version 0.10.0 and newer\n- Some features unavailable on older brokers\n- Will throw `UnsupportedVersionException` if using unsupported feature\n\n---\n\n## Performance Tuning\n\n### For Higher Throughput\n\n- Increase `fetch.min.bytes` (wait for more data)\n- Increase `fetch.max.wait.ms` (batch more fetches)\n- Increase `max.poll.records` (larger batches)\n- Decrease `max.partition.fetch.bytes` to reduce per-request size\n\n### For Lower Latency\n\n- Decrease `fetch.min.bytes`\n- Decrease `fetch.max.wait.ms`\n- Decrease `max.poll.records`\n- Increase `connections` and pipeline requests\n\n### For Stable Consumption\n\n- Increase `max.poll.interval.ms` if processing is variable\n- Decrease `heartbeat.interval.ms` relative to `session.timeout.ms` (e.g., 3000:45000)\n- Ensure polling frequency > 1 / (max.poll.interval.ms / 1000)\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe KafkaConsumer provides a flexible, powerful API for consuming messages from Kafka. Key principles:\n\n1. **Consumer groups** distribute partitions and provide automatic failover\n2. **Two offset concepts**: position (current) and committed (saved)\n3. **Rebalance callbacks** coordinate state around partition changes\n4. **poll()** is the main event loop; everything happens during poll\n5. **Not thread-safe** except wakeup(); use proper synchronization\n6. **Careful offset management** is critical for correctness\n7. **Configuration drives behavior** significantly; understand key parameters\n\nFor production systems, implement proper error handling, offset management strategy, monitoring, and graceful shutdown patterns.\n",

# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer API Reference Documentation

## Overview

The `KafkaConsumer` is a client for consuming messages from Apache Kafka topics. It transparently handles broker failures and topic partition migration while managing consumer group coordination for load-balanced consumption. The consumer maintains TCP connections to brokers and must be properly closed to avoid resource leaks.

**Thread Safety Model**: The KafkaConsumer is **NOT thread-safe**. All network I/O occurs in the thread making the call. The only thread-safe method is `wakeup()`, which can safely interrupt blocking operations from external threads.

## Core Consumer Lifecycle

### Constructors

#### `KafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)`
Creates a consumer with a configuration map. Configuration keys are documented in `ConsumerConfig`.

**Parameters:**
- `configs`: Map of configuration key-value pairs

**Throws:**
- `KafkaException`: If consumer construction fails (invalid configuration, missing deserializers, etc.)
